#Paleo Plantain Chips

Ingredients:

1 green plantain
1 Tblsp coconut oil mixed with #ghee, melted
Â½ tsp pink Himalayan salt {or more to your liking}
Directions:

Heat oven to 350Â° F. 
Cut the ends off and then score the length of the plantain with about three evenly spaced cuts. Donâ€™t cut too far into the flesh, you just want to cut through the skin.
Peel the plantain then slice it on a diagonal as thinly as you can consistently manage.
Toss the plantain slices with the melted oil, lay out on the baking sheet(increased/unlined), and sprinkle with the salt.
Bake for 15 minutes.
{Leave in longer or shorter depending on how your oven heats and feel free to remove the more well-done chips as they start to brown.} Enjoy! ğŸŒâ¤ï¸"

Comment: viirdii said "Hi ladies and gents! This is a fast Contour and highlighting video for you all. This is my technique and I hope it helps in some kind of wayğŸ˜Š. I wish I could have a full video up but soon I will be making long and detailed videos on my YT channel.  This is it for now, I hope you guys enjoy!ğŸ˜˜ PRODUCTS USED***
-1. I applied my favorite drug store foundation from @lorealparisusa (Visible Lift Blur in  Sun Beige 210 and Light Ivory 201)
-2. I start the contour and highlight process, I begin applying a highlight foundation and a contour foundation from the @bhcosmetics foundation and concealer 10 color palette 1&2. ( I have both) -3. I then apply the highlighting foundation where you see the lightest on my face and with that I apply my favorite concealer L.A girl pro conceal by @lagirlcosmetics . Then I apply the contour foundation where you see the darkest on my face.
-4. Remember highlighting is where you want places and features on your face to stand out as suppose to contour are places and features you wish to Shrink or hide.
-5. After you have that you either want to blend with a buffing brush (anytime of brush that you think might work, works too) or my favorite, a beauty blender. -6. Once everything is set and well blended you want to set your highlight and contour with similar colors as your highlight and contour foundations or concealers. This will prevent oiliness and prevents your makeup from going everywhere. -7. Once that is done you are basically done! ----- #Amrezy #anastasiabeverlyhills #beautyguru #beautyblogger #glamherbooth #hudabeauty #inssta_makeup #Mua #motd #vegas_nay #vanitymakeup #wakeupandmakeup #beauty #makeupfanatic1 #Ghalichiglam #lillyghalichi #lagirlcosmetics #ardell #ardelllashes #WetNWild #iluvsarahii #makeupgeekcosmetics #violetvoss #laurag_143 #nyxcosmetics #morphebrushes #elf #makeup #MakeupByViiRDii #bhcosmetics -----"

Comment: realfood_realfit said "While exercise is certainly part of the formula for success, the foods you choose to eat are 3x more important for controlling your weight than your exercise. 
It's very easy to sabotage yourself with processed foods & sweetened beverages. Research suggests getting enough fiber may be a key component for effective weight loss. 
Simply upping your fiber intake may actually help you achieve results rivaling more complicated diets. Previous research has demonstrated that fiber has appetite-suppressant qualities that helps you feel more satiated, thereby preventing unhealthy snacking.

Dietary guidelines call for 20-30 grams of fiber per day. I believe an ideal amount for most adults is around 32 grams daily. Most people, however, get only half that, or lessâ€”despite the fact that most eat a diet high in grains. 
Many whole foods, especially fruits and vegetables, naturally contain bothsoluble and insoluble fiber. This is ideal, as both help feed the microorganisms living in your gut. These beneficial bacteria in turn assist with digestion and absorption of your food, and play a significant role in your immune function. 
So, to maximize your health benefits, focus on eating more vegetables, nuts, and seeds. Following is a small sampling of foods that contain high levels of soluble and insoluble fiber. 
Psyllium seed husk, flax, and chia seeds, Berries, Vegetables such as broccoli and Brussels sprouts, Root vegetables and tubers, including onions, sweet potatoes, and jicama, Almonds, Peas, Green beans, Cauliflower, Beans. 
A simple tip to increase the amount of #fiber and biodense nutrients in your diet would be to add sunflower sprouts to your meal. They work great in salads but can also be added to virtually any dish to radically improve its nutrition."

Comment: realfood_realfit said "While exercise is certainly part of the formula for success, the foods you choose to eat are 3x more important for controlling your weight than your exercise. 
It's very easy to sabotage yourself with processed foods & sweetened beverages. Research suggests getting enough fiber may be a key component for effective weight loss. 
Simply upping your fiber intake may actually help you achieve results rivaling more complicated diets. Previous research has demonstrated that fiber has appetite-suppressant qualities that helps you feel more satiated, thereby preventing unhealthy snacking.

Dietary guidelines call for 20-30 grams of fiber per day. I believe an ideal amount for most adults is around 32 grams daily. Most people, however, get only half that, or lessâ€”despite the fact that most eat a diet high in grains. 
Many whole foods, especially fruits and vegetables, naturally contain bothsoluble and insoluble fiber. This is ideal, as both help feed the microorganisms living in your gut. These beneficial bacteria in turn assist with digestion and absorption of your food, and play a significant role in your immune function. 
So, to maximize your health benefits, focus on eating more vegetables, nuts, and seeds. Following is a small sampling of foods that contain high levels of soluble and insoluble fiber. 
Psyllium seed husk, flax, and chia seeds, Berries, Vegetables such as broccoli and Brussels sprouts, Root vegetables and tubers, including onions, sweet potatoes, and jicama, Almonds, Peas, Green beans, Cauliflower, Beans. 
A simple tip to increase the amount of #fiber and biodense nutrients in your diet would be to add sunflower sprouts to your meal. They work great in salads but can also be added to virtually any dish to radically improve its nutrition."
